Section 1:
SECOND REGULAR SESSION
103RD GENERAL ASSEMBLY
INTRODUCED BY REPRESENTATIVE DAVIS.
7230H.01I JOSEPH ENGLER, Chief Clerk
AN ACT
To repeal sections 128.345, 128.346, and 128.348, RSMo, and to enact in lieu thereof eleven
new sections relating to the composition of congressional districts.
Be it enacted by the General Assembly of the state of Missouri, as follows:

Section 2:
Section A. Sections 128.345, 128.346, and 128.348, RSMo, are repealed and eleven
2 new sections enacted in lieu thereof, to be known as sections 128.345, 128.346, 128.348,
3 128.481, 128.482, 128.483, 128.484, 128.485, 128.486, 128.487, and 128.488, to read as
4 follows:

Section 3:
128.345. 1. All references in sections 128.451 to 128.458 to counties, voting districts
2 (VTD), and tract-blocks (Block) mean those counties, voting districts (VTD), and tract-blocks
3 (Block) as reported to the state by the United States Bureau of the Census for the 2010 census.
4 2. All references in sections 128.461 to [128.478] 128.488to counties, voting districts
5 (VTD), and tract-blocks (Block) mean those counties, voting districts (VTD), and tract-blocks
6 (Block) as reported to the state by the United States Bureau of the Census for the 2020 census.

Section 4:
128.346. 1. The districts established by the provisions of sections 128.400 to 128.440
2 for the election of representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective
3 beginning with election to the 108th Congress and through the election of the 112th Congress.
4 2. The districts established by sections 128.451 to 128.458 for the election of
5 representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective beginning with the
6 election to the 113th Congress and through the election of the 117th Congress.
7 3. The districts established by sections 128.461 to 128.468 for the election of
8 representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective beginning with the
9 election to the 118th Congress and through the election of the 119th Congress.
EXPLANATION — Matter enclosed in bold-faced brackets [thus] in the above bill is not enacted and is
intended to be omitted from the law. Matter in bold-face type in the above bill is proposed language.
HB 3487 2
10 4. The districts established by sections 128.471 to 128.478 for the election of
11 representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective [beginning with] forthe
12 election of the 120th Congress.
13 5. The district established by sections 128.481 to 128.488 for the election of
14 representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective beginning with the
15 election of the 121st Congress.

Section 5:
128.348. 1. Effective with the election for the 113th Congress and through the
2 election of the 117th Congress, the state of Missouri shall consist of eight congressional
3 districts.
4 2. Effective with the election of the 118th Congress, the state of Missouri shall consist
5 of eight congressional districts.
6 3. Effective with the election of the 120th Congress, the state of Missouri shall consist
7 of eight congressional districts.
8 4. Effective with the election of the 121st Congress, the state of Missouri shall
9 consist of eight congressional districts.
10 [4.] 5. The legal voters of each district shall elect one member of Congress of the
11 United States.

Raw Text:
SECOND REGULAR SESSION
HOUSE BILL NO. 3487
103RD GENERAL ASSEMBLY
INTRODUCED BY REPRESENTATIVE DAVIS.
7230H.01I JOSEPH ENGLER, Chief Clerk
AN ACT
To repeal sections 128.345, 128.346, and 128.348, RSMo, and to enact in lieu thereof eleven
new sections relating to the composition of congressional districts.
Be it enacted by the General Assembly of the state of Missouri, as follows:
Section A. Sections 128.345, 128.346, and 128.348, RSMo, are repealed and eleven
2 new sections enacted in lieu thereof, to be known as sections 128.345, 128.346, 128.348,
3 128.481, 128.482, 128.483, 128.484, 128.485, 128.486, 128.487, and 128.488, to read as
4 follows:
128.345. 1. All references in sections 128.451 to 128.458 to counties, voting districts
2 (VTD), and tract-blocks (Block) mean those counties, voting districts (VTD), and tract-blocks
3 (Block) as reported to the state by the United States Bureau of the Census for the 2010 census.
4 2. All references in sections 128.461 to [128.478] 128.488to counties, voting districts
5 (VTD), and tract-blocks (Block) mean those counties, voting districts (VTD), and tract-blocks
6 (Block) as reported to the state by the United States Bureau of the Census for the 2020 census.
128.346. 1. The districts established by the provisions of sections 128.400 to 128.440
2 for the election of representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective
3 beginning with election to the 108th Congress and through the election of the 112th Congress.
4 2. The districts established by sections 128.451 to 128.458 for the election of
5 representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective beginning with the
6 election to the 113th Congress and through the election of the 117th Congress.
7 3. The districts established by sections 128.461 to 128.468 for the election of
8 representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective beginning with the
9 election to the 118th Congress and through the election of the 119th Congress.
EXPLANATION — Matter enclosed in bold-faced brackets [thus] in the above bill is not enacted and is
intended to be omitted from the law. Matter in bold-face type in the above bill is proposed language.

HB 3487 2
10 4. The districts established by sections 128.471 to 128.478 for the election of
11 representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective [beginning with] forthe
12 election of the 120th Congress.
13 5. The district established by sections 128.481 to 128.488 for the election of
14 representatives to the Congress of the United States shall be effective beginning with the
15 election of the 121st Congress.
128.348. 1. Effective with the election for the 113th Congress and through the
2 election of the 117th Congress, the state of Missouri shall consist of eight congressional
3 districts.
4 2. Effective with the election of the 118th Congress, the state of Missouri shall consist
5 of eight congressional districts.
6 3. Effective with the election of the 120th Congress, the state of Missouri shall consist
7 of eight congressional districts.
8 4. Effective with the election of the 121st Congress, the state of Missouri shall
9 consist of eight congressional districts.
10 [4.] 5. The legal voters of each district shall elect one member of Congress of the
11 United States.
